           Neu: Die Adobe Stock Premium Collection
          </span>
         </h3>
         <div class="margin-bottom-large">
          <p class="no-margin">
           <span class="grey mountain-mist-text text-large light" data-t="premium-description">
            Inspirierende Bilder von ausgewählten Adobe Stock-Anbietern entdecken
           </span>
          </p>
         </div>
        </div>
        <div class="margin-bottom-xlarge">
         <div class="padding-bottom-medium">
          <a class="button button--action button--silent" data-t="premium-discover-collections-button-text" href="/de/premium">

          </a>

    <script type="text/javascript">
     var hero_image = document.getElementsByClassName('js-hero-image')[0],
             hero_image_url = "https://as.ftcdn.net/r/v1/pics/554718212b0b45980be3752dcf188f203b6d8e04/home/1555/1555-hero-toys.jpg";
 
     if (hero_image && hero_image.classList.contains('blurry-image')) {
         var img = new Image();
         img.onload = function() {
             hero_image.style.backgroundImage = 'url(' + hero_image_url + ')';
             hero_image.classList.remove('blurry-image');
             hero_image.classList.add('animated-image');
         }
         img.src = hero_image_url;
     }
    </script>

          <h3 class="no-margin">
           <span class="text-up text-sregular bold enhanced-tracking" data-t="integration-title">
            Schneller arbeiten
           </span>
          </h3>
         </div>
         <div class="margin-bottom-large">
          <p class="no-margin">
           <span class="grey mountain-mist-text text-large light" data-t="integration-description1">
            Finden Sie das perfekte Bild für Ihr nächstes Kreativprojekt.
           </span>
          </p>
          <p class="no-margin">
           <span class="grey mountain-mist-text text-large light" data-t="integration-description2">
            Direkt in Ihren Adobe Creative Cloud-Applikationen.
           </span>
          </p>
         </div>
         <div class="row">
          <div class="column on-small-12 on-medium-2 on-medium-offset-5">
           <div class="border-top-1 border-solid silver-sand-border">
           </div>
          </div>
         </div>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <div class="padding-top-large">
       <div class="padding-xlarge">
        <div class="container-max center-align">
         <img alt="open in example" class="responsive-img" data-t="integration-open-in-image" src="https://as.ftcdn.net/r/v1/pics/a014e23bc2f86a494c2eb15c032c51a3b120c2d7/home/open-in.jpg"/>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <div class="padding-left-xlarge padding-right-xlarge">
       <div class="container-max">
        <div class="row">
         <div class="column on-small-12 on-large-4">
          <div class="padding-top-xlarge padding-bottom-large">
           <p class="no-margin">
            <span class="grey mountain-mist-text text-large light" data-t="integration-paragraph1-text">
             Verwenden Sie in Ihren Designs zur Vorschau zunächst Bilder mit Wasserzeichen. Lizenzierung, Zugriff und Verwaltung sind dann direkt in Photoshop CC, InDesign CC, Illustrator CC oder einer anderen Adobe-Desktop-Applikation möglich.
            </span>

    <script type="text/javascript">
     var hero_image = document.getElementsByClassName('js-hero-image')[0],
             hero_image_url = "https://as.ftcdn.net/r/v1/pics/554718212b0b45980be3752dcf188f203b6d8e04/home/1555/1555-hero-toys.jpg";
 
     if (hero_image && hero_image.classList.contains('blurry-image')) {
         var img = new Image();
         img.onload = function() {
             hero_image.style.backgroundImage = 'url(' + hero_image_url + ')';
             hero_image.classList.remove('blurry-image');
             hero_image.classList.add('animated-image');
         }
         img.src = hero_image_url;
     }
    </script>
